27a3(mdo sde): thos ma thag tu mo mtshan mi snang bar gyur te/ pho mtshan skyes nas de dag thams cad bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi logs par gyur te/ thams
27a4(mdo sde): cad kyang ma 'ongs pa na bud med kyi dngos po thob par 'gyur ba'i las kyi sgrib pa ma lus par byang nas/ dang bud med de dag thams cad kyis thal mo sbyar te/ de
27a5(mdo sde): bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa de la phyag 'tshal zhing 'di skad ces gsol to// de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
27a6(mdo sde): shAkya thub pa ngo mtshar mdzad pa la phyag 'tshal lo// phyag 'tshal lo// thugs rje chen po gang gis bdag cag da ltar bud med kyi dngos po mi gda' bar gyur cing / 
27a7(mdo sde): rnam pa thams cad rdzogs pa'i skyes pa'i dngos por gyur pa'i sngon byung ba 'di rgya cher bshad du gsol/ de lta bu'i ngo mtshar dang / cho phrul dang / skyob pas bdag cag bla na med pa
27a8(mdo sde): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems skyes par bgyi'o// bcom ldan 'das sngon byung ba 'di lha dang mi dpag tu ma mchis pa rnams dbang du 'gyur bar bshad du
27b1(mdo sde): gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas sngon byung ba 'di bshad pa ni/ bzhin bzangs dag gang gi tshe de bzhin gshegs pa 'od ni spros snang dpal de'i
27b2(mdo sde): zad nas rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong gi btsun mo dam pa lha mdzes bud med brgyad khri bzhi stong dang bcas pas rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di thos te thos ma thag tu btsun mo dam pa lha mdzes
27b3(mdo sde): dang bud med brgyad khri bzhi stong de dag mo mtshan mi snang bar gyur te/ po mtshan skyes pa de'i tshe/ de bzhin du lha'i bu mo'i bar du grangs med dpag tu med pa dag rin po tog gi gzungs 'di
27b4(mdo sde): thos ma thag tu bud med kyi dbang po mi snang bar gyur nas/ skyes pa'i dbang po skyes ste/ bud med de dag thams cad ma 'ongs pa na bud med kyi dngos po thob par 'gyur
27b5(mdo sde): ba'i las kyi sgrib pa ma lus par byang ngo // gang gi tshe rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong gi btsun mo dam pa lha mdzes btsun mo'i 'khor dang bcas pa phor gyur pa
27b6(mdo sde): de'i rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong des bu thu bo gling bzhi la 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal por dbang bskur bas dbang bskur te/ bu stong du gcig gi ma tshang ba dang / skyes bu chen
27b7(mdo sde): po lha mdzes dang bcas// lha mdzes kyang skyes bu chen po brgyad khri bzhi stong dang bcas gzhan yang srog chags dgu khri nyis stong dang bcas te khyim nas byung nas/ de bzhin gsheg/ 
27b8(mdo sde): pa 'od ni spos snang dpal de'i thad du skra dang kha spu dregs gos ngur smrig bgos te/ yang dag par dad pas khyim nas khyim med par rab tu byung ngo // rab tu byung nas kha ton
28a1(mdo sde): la dga' zhing tshul bzhin yid la byed pa la brtson par gyur to// de nas de na srog chags bye ba mang po 'di snyam du sems te/ de ci'i phyir 'khor long/ 
28a2(mdo sde): sbyar ba'i rgyal po rab tu byung snyam nas/ de dag phan tshun 'di skad smra'o// dge sbyong 'di ni bdud kyi las la brtson pa ste/ g.yon can sgyu ma bdud kyi las dang ldan pas chos
28a3(mdo sde): 'di ston cing la la ni po mtshan med par byas la la ni mo mtshan med par byas/ la la ni skra dang kha spu bregs/ la la ni gos tshon can bskon/ la lA ni gos dkar po bskon/ la la
28a4(mdo sde): ni lhar skye bar chos ston// la la ni mir skyo bar la la ni dud 'gro'i gnas su skye bar/ la la ni yi dgas su skye bar/ la la ni sems can dmyal bar skye bar la la
28a5(mdo sde): ni shi 'pho dang / skye ba med par bya bar chos ston te bdud/ kyi las la brtson zhing bud med sbyar ba'i sgra dang ldan pa/ dge sbyong 'od zhi spos snang dpal de dge sbyong gi gzugs
28a6(mdo sde): kyi rab tu slu ba yin gyis bdag cag 'di nas dong ste/ de'i gzugs dang rtags 'dzin pa yang mi mthong ba dang / de'i tshig kyang cung zad kyang mi thos par 'dong ngo // de nas de nyid na shor ba
28a7(mdo sde): gzhon nu'i tshul zhes bya ba zhig yod pa de tshig 'di skad ces smras so// kho bo'i chung ma dang / g.yog mo dang / bu mo gang yin pa de dag thams cad kyang / dge sbyong ma rungs pa 'dis
28a8(mdo sde): mo mtshan med par byas te/ skyes pa'i dbang por sprul nas thams cad kyi mgo bregs te/ gos tshon can bson nas/ kho bo gcig pu mya ngan gyis non te/ 
28b1(mdo sde): tha na bdag cag thams cad 'dus la gang du dge sbyong ma rungs pa dang / dge sbyong sgyu ma bdud kyi zhags pa la brtson pa 'di'i sgra dang / skad kyi mi thos na mthong ba lta smos kyang ci dgos
28b2(mdo sde): pa'i ri khrod nyams ngabar 'dong gis/ tshur shog ces byas pa dang // de dag thams cad dga' ste de bzhin no zhes zer ro// de nas shor ba bzhon nu'i tshul dang the tsom du gyur pa
28b3(mdo sde): srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong mang po lhan cig tu de nas dong ste/ yul mtha' 'khob ri khrod nyam nga bar drang srong gi cha byad kyis spyod pa spyod cing // sems can de dag la 'di skad ces
28b4(mdo sde): chos ston to// 'khor ba las thar pa yang med legs par byas pa dang / nyes par byas pa'i las kyi 'bros bu rnam par smin pa snga med na/ der chad par
28b5(mdo sde): smra ba'i dge sbyong bdud kyi las kyi lam la brtson pa zhig byung gis/ gang dag de la lta ba'i phyir 'gro ba dang / gang dag gus par smra ba dang / gang dag de'i chos nyan pa de
28b6(mdo sde): dag sems g.yengs pa yin de dag mgo bregs khyim nas phyung gos tshon can bskon dur khrod du spyad pa spyod du bcug/ slobs mo pa'i spyod pa la btsud/ zan za cig par byed/ 
28b7(mdo sde): lta ba mi bzad pa'i yid ldan pa dang / rtag tu yid 'byung bar byed// dben par gnas pa la dga' ba dang / gnas khang du bcug/ 'dod pa'i dga' ba glu gar dang / drang ba/ 
28b8(mdo sde): dang dri dang / byug pa dang / rgyan dang / lhang lbub dang / 'khrig pa'i chos dang / chang dang / ra ro bar 'gyur ba'i btung ba spangs shing smra ba nyung bar byed/ 
29a1(mdo sde): de lta bur dge sbyong gi gzugs kyis chad par smra ba bdud kyis chad par las la brtson pa de sems can rnams kyi dgrar gyur pa zhig byung ste/ dge sbyong go'u tam de'i
29a2(mdo sde): byed pa ni sngon ma thos ma mthong ba yin pa kho bos rtogs so zhes de srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong mang po de lta bu'i sdig pa can gyi lta ba 'dzin du bcug go// de nas dus gzhan zhig na
29a3(mdo sde): dge sbyong chen po ud pa la'i gdong gis thos pa gshed kyi ri khrod na/ kha cig bdag nyid kyang lam ngan par zhugs shing gzhan yang lta ba mi bzad pa 'dzin du bcug ste/ dkon mchog
29a4(mdo sde): gsum la mi snyan pa sgrogs so zhes thos nas de 'di snyam du sems so// bdag gis semasacan 'di dag sdig pa'i lta ba las yongs su thar par ma byas
29a5(mdo sde): shing yang dag par lta ba la ma bkod na/ bdag dge sbyong du gyur pa don med do// ma 'ongs pa'i dus na ldongs par gyur pa'i 'jig rten du bdag ji ltar bla na med
29a6(mdo sde): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bya/ ji ltar rab tu nyam zag par gyur pa bdud bzhi'i zhags pa'i bcing bas cings pa'i sems can
29a7(mdo sde): rnams yongs su dgrol bar nus snyam ste/ de nas dge sbyong chen po ud pa la'i gdong brtul ba che zhing brtan pa/ snying rje chen po dang ldan pas de bzhin gshegs pa 'od zhi spos
29a8(mdo sde): snang dpal la zhus te/ srog chags brgya stong du mas bskor cing 'dun bdar nas/ mtha' 'khob kyi grong dang / grong khyer dang / grong rdal dang / ri dang / ri brag
29b1(mdo sde): nyam nga ba'i gnas de dang de dag na spyad pa spyod cing / de dang de dag tu sems can de dag la ci nas sems can de dag sdig pa'i lta bar song ba las zlog ste/ yang dag pa'i lta ba la btsud
29b2(mdo sde): nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu bkod/ gzhan la la ni rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa la smon// la la ni nyan thos kyi theg pa la/ la la 'bras bu la
29b3(mdo sde): bkod/ la la ni rab tu byung / la la ni dge bsnyen gyi sdom pa la// la la ni za cig pa la/ la la ni skyabs gsum du 'gro ba la bkod pa de lta bur chos ston to// bud med
29b4(mdo sde): dag ni rin po che tog gi gzungs 'di bshad de bud med kyi dngos po las sgyur nas skyes pa la bkod do// srog chags mang po gang dag de bzhin gshegs pa
29b5(mdo sde): la the tsom du gyur pa de dag thams cad kyang sdig pa'ilta bar song ba de las bzlog ste/ nyes pa chags su bcug nas// bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs
29b6(mdo sde): pa'i byang chub la bkod de/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'od zhi spos snang dpal de nyid la phul nas rab tu phyung ngo // shor ba gzhon nu'i tshul ni ma btogs ste/ des 'di ltar ud
29b7(mdo sde): pa la'i gdong 'di bdag gi 'khor rnams bslus te khrid kyis bdag gis kyang 'di bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa'i zhing dar bdud
29b8(mdo sde): byas te/ 'di ltar mngal na 'dug pa tshun chad 'di la rnam par gtse'o// de nas phyis btsas nas kyang gzhon nu rtsed mo byed pa dang / bzo'i las kyi mtha' dang / klog cing / 
30a1(mdo sde): 'dug pa dang / dga' ba'i rtsed mo'i phyir btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang du song ba nas/ byang chub kyi shing drung du byang chub kyi snying po la 'dug gi bar du skrag par bya'o// 
30a2(mdo sde): bgegs bya'o// byang chub thob nas kyang bstan pa gzhig par bya'o// zhes smon lam btab bo// de nas dge sbyong chen po ud pa la'i gdong gis shor ba gzhon nu'i tshul gyis smon
30a3(mdo sde): lam de ltar brtul te btab pa la mthu chen po dang 'bad pa drag pos dad par byas te/ sdig pa'i lta ba'i thibs po de las bzlog nas nyes pa 'chags su bcug ste/ bla na med pa
30a4(mdo sde): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyesadu bcug go/ de nas shor ba gzhon nu'i tshul rab tu dul zhing dad pa skyes nas/ 'di skad du snying rje
30a5(mdo sde): chen po dang ldan pa khyod gang gi tshe/ bla na med pa yang / dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa de'i tshe/ byang chub thob nas bdag
30a6(mdo sde): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lung bstan tu gsol zhes smon lam btab bo// bzhin bzangs dag de'i tshe de'i dus na/ gang gis de bzhin gshegs pa 'od zhi
30a7(mdo sde): spos snang dpal de 'khor dang bcas pa la mchod pa dang / rim 'gro rnam pa du ma byas nas srog chags bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma dang bcas te mngon par byung na/ rab tu byung zhing
30a8(mdo sde): srog chag bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du ma ni sdig pa'i lta bar song ba las bzlog ste/ theg pa gsum la bkod/ sems can dpag tu med pa ni 'bras bu la bkod/ bud
30b1(mdo sde): med bye ba khrug khrig brgya stong tshad med pa ni skyes pa thob par byas pa'i rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong zhes bya bar 'gyur ba de gzhan zhig yin snyam du khyed be tsom 'am/ yid gnyis
30b2(mdo sde): sam/ som nyi za bar gyur na de ltar mi blta'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ da de'i tshe de'i dus na gleng bzhi la dbang ba'i 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po ud pa la'i gdong zhes bya bar
30b3(mdo sde): gyur te/ ngas de lta bu'i skyes bu'i 'thu byaso// bzhin bzangs dag de'i tshe de'i dus na/ btsun mo dam pa lha mdzes shes bya ba gang gi dge sbyong thob par gyur pa de gzhan
30b4(mdo sde): yin snyam du khyod the tsom 'am/ yid gnyis sam/ som nyi za bar gyur na da ltar mi blta'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems
30b5(mdo sde): dpa' chen po byams pa de'i tshe de'i dus na/ btsun mo dam pa lha mdzes shes bya bar gyur to// bzhin bzangs dag de'i tshe de'i dus na/ the tsom du gyur pa'i
30b6(mdo sde): srog chags bye ba mang po dang bcas/ sangs rgyas la mi snyan pa'i bar du zer shor ba gzhon nu'i tshul zhes bya ba de gzhan yin snyam du khyed the tshom 'am/ yid gnyis sam/ 
30b7(mdo sde): som nyi za bar gyur na de ltar mi blta'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ bdud sdig can 'di nyid de'i tshe de'i dus na shor ba gzhon nu'i tshul zhes bya bar gyur te/ gang de'i tshe
30b8(mdo sde): ngas de'i 'khor rab tu byung bas de'i phyir nga la sems rab tu khro ba bskyed nas/ phyis smon lam btab te/ khyod nam bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon
31a1(mdo sde): par rdzogs par sangs rgyas pa de'i me khyod kyis bdag blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sung ston cig ces byang so// rigs
31a2(mdo sde): bu dag khyod kyis kyang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa 'od zhi spos snang dpal de la ma dad cing ma bsdams pa'i tshig smras te/ sdig pa'i lta bar song ba bzung nas/ ngas
31a3(mdo sde): khyad sdig pa'i lta bar song ba de las kun thar par byas te rab tu phyung bas de tshun chad khyed kyis sangs rgyas brgya stong mang po la bsnyen bskur byas te/ de dag la mchod pa dang / 
31a4(mdo sde): rim gro byas/ de dag las chos mnyan te smon de lam btab nas pha rol tu phyin pa drug spyod do// khyed lus dang / dag dang yid kyis nyes pa spyad pa'i las
31a5(mdo sde): des sngon bskal pa du mar ngan song gsum du sdug bsngal myong ngo // las kyi sgrib pa de nyid kyis da ltar bdud sdig can gyi gnas su skyes so// rin
31a6(mdo sde): po che tog gi gzungs sngon byung ba'i le'u 'di bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas bshad pa na/ bdud kyi bu mo lnga brgya tsam de dag bud med kyi dngos po/ 
31a7(mdo sde): mi snang bar gyur nas/ skyes pa'i dngos por gyur te// mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa thob bo// lha dang / mi dang / lha ma yin du bcas pa'i skye dgu'i sems can bya ba khrag khrig brgya
31a8(mdo sde): stong grangs med dpag tu med pa dag gis ni/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems skyed de/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi
31b1(mdo sde): ldog par gyur to// de bzhin du sems can bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med dpag tu med pa dag ni/ nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi theg pa las phyir mi ldog par gyur/ 
31b2(mdo sde): to// lha dang / mi'i bu mo grangs med dpag tu med pa dag ni bud med kyi dngos po las gyur te/ skyes pa'i dngos po rnyed do// 'dus pa chen po rin po che rtog gi gzungs las
31b3(mdo sde): sngon byung ba'i le'u ste gnyis pa'o// de nas rin po tog gi gzungs 'di de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pas bshad pa de'i tshe/ thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khan
31b4(mdo sde): mi mdzad 'di rgya cher snang bas khyab par gyur te/ sangs rgyas kyis zhing 'di na gling bzhi pa bye ba phrag brgya gang yod pa de dag na 'dod pa'i dbang phyug bdud
31b5(mdo sde): bye ba phrag brgya gang dag bdud bye ba de dag sangs rgyas/ kyi mthus dogs pa skyes te/ snang ba chen po 'di/ gang nas byung zhes gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di
31b6(mdo sde): la lta zhing bdud sdig can zhes bya ba gang gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams de na gnas pa de bdag cag pas stobs che zhing dbang tshal mthu chen 'di de'i mthu'am snyam nas
31b7(mdo sde): de nas bdud de dag gis bltas na/ bdud sdig can de mya ngan gyi khang pa na 'dug cing yid rab tu mi dga' ba de mthong ngo // de nas bdud bye ba phrag brgya po de dag gling bzhi pa'i
31b8(mdo sde): 'jig rten gyi khams 'di dag ga la ba dang / bdud sdig can gyi khang pa ga la ba der dong ste phyin nas/ bdud sdig can la 'di skad ces smras so// kye 'dod pa'i dbang phyug ci'i phyir thams
32a1(mdo sde): cad dang ldan pa'i gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di snang bar byas nas/ khyod mya ngan gyi khang par zhugs te 'dug/ de nas 'dod pa'i dbang
32a2(mdo sde): byug gis bdud bye ba phrag brgya po de dag la rgyas par smras pa/ kye grogs po dag shes par gyis shig/ shAkya'i rigs las shin tu g.yo dang / sbyar ldan pa'i dge sbyong zhig
32a3(mdo sde): 'dir skyes te/ de skyes ma thag tu thams cad dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di snang bar byas/ rab tu g.yos par byas/ 'khrugs par byas te/ spangs par byas
32a4(mdo sde): so// 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa 'di na mkhas pa gang su tshangs pa'i dbang po 'am klu'i dbang po'am/ gnod sbyin gyi dbang po 'am/ 
32a5(mdo sde): ma yin gyi dbang po 'am/ lto 'phye chen po'i dbang po'am/ na mkha' lding gi dbang po 'am/ mi 'am ci'i dbang po nas gzhan yang mi dang mi ma
32a6(mdo sde): yin pa'i bar du mkhas pa su yang rung / de dag thams cad de la mchod pa'i phyir dong ngo // lo drug gi bar du gcig pu gnyis su med par 'dug ste/ mtshan nyid med pa'i
32a7(mdo sde): sgyu ma bsgrubs pas kho bos kyang rang gi stobs kun bstan par 'dod na/ sde dang g.yog bye ba phrag sum cu rtsa drug dag de'i drung du dong ste/ kun tu bskor nas bdud kyi stobs
32a8(mdo sde): dang rnam par 'phrul pa dang / rdzu 'phrul dang / brtson 'grus dang / pha rol gnon pa thams cad bstan kyang de'i spu'i khung bu gcig kyang sngangs shing 'jig par bya ma
32b1(mdo sde): nus na/ stan de las spyod pa lta ci smos bgegs gzhan bya bar ga la nus te/ mdangs gsum des de lta bu'i sgra shin tu bstan cings g.yo bar byas pas kho bo lnga
32b2(mdo sde): dang bcas de pham nas shing bcad pa bzhin du sa'i steng du lhung ngo // de der 'dug ste de 'dra ba'i mtshan nyid med pa'i sgyu ma bsgrubs nas/ 'di ltar bdud kyi yul thams cad zil
32b3(mdo sde): gyis mnan te/ rig pa bsgrubs nas stan de las langs te/ sems can rnams la rab tu bstan nas gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di na sems can su mkhas shing shes
32b4(mdo sde): pa de dag kyang de lta bu'i sgyu mas 'dun par byas te/ de dag gi sems dang 'gro ba drug du skye ba dang / 'gro ba kho bos ma shes so// gang dag de la skyabs su dong ba
32b5(mdo sde): de dag gi spu'i khung bu gcig tsam yang sngangs pa dang 'khrugapar kho bos byed mi nus na/ de las sru ba'am/ bskyod par ltag la nus/ dang kho bos g.yog mo lnga
32b6(mdo sde): brgya dang bu nyi khri'i tshogs kyi 'khor dang bcas te dge sbyong go'u ta ma mdangs de la skyabs su dong nas/ chos nyan pa'i phyir de'i mdun na 'khod de/ kho bos de dag de dang dbral
32b7(mdo sde): ma nus so// de'i phyir stobs dang ldan pa/ bsod nams dang ldan pa// shes rab dang ldan pa/ dbang phyug dang ldan pa khyed kho bo'i grogs kyis shAkya'i bu mdangs te srog dang
32b8(mdo sde): dpral lo// de la sems can gang dag skyabs su dong ba de dag thams cad kyang rnam par bzhig par bya'o// dge sbyong g.yo rgyu can nag po'i phyogs pham par byas te/ bdud kyi phyogs
33a1(mdo sde): dkar po snang bar byas la// de phyin chad bde ba la gnas par bya'o// de nas bdud me 'od ces bya bas 'dzam bu'i gling 'di gang na de bzhin gshegs
33a2(mdo sde): pa bzhugs shing chos 'chad pa la bltas pa dang / de nas bdud me 'od kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi sku mthong sgra dbyangs dang ldan pa'i chos bstan pa thos so// thos nas da
33a3(mdo sde): spu zing zhes byed cing spangs par gyur te/ de nas des bdud sdig can de la 'di skad ces smras so// ma lus zhing na 'di ni gzugs bzang mchog/ bsod nams shes pas
33a4(mdo sde): ring nas gtsang ste// nyon mongs rnam grol lam ldan yun ring lon// srid pa kun zad mya ngan rnam sa las thar// khyod yang mi rigs khro ba'i dbang ma
33a5(mdo sde): 'gro/ gtso mchog 'di ni srid pa gsum na skyabs// 'di la zhe sdang cung zad su bskyed pa// da ni rmongs shing bde ba nyams par 'gyur// de nas gzhan
33a6(mdo sde): yang bdud mu khyud bzang po zhes bya bas bdud sdig can de la 'di skad ces smras so// de ni 'phrul chen bsod nams rab kyi mtshan// mi gnas 'gro ba kun las rab tu thar/ 
33a7(mdo sde): sdug bsngal ma lus zad pa'i lam ston pa// bdud brgya kun gyis gtse bar bya mi nus// sdig can gyis smras pa// nga yi skye bo dag la dbang byas te// khyod kyi skye bo 'di
33a8(mdo sde): de dbang 'gro// de yis ring por mi thogs yul stongs bya// yu bu cag kyang gong du 'gro bar 'gyur// de nas bdud nags kyi rgyal po zhes bya ba des 'di skad ces smras so// khyod
33b1(mdo sde): ni rab tu 'byor par gyur pa'i tshe/ de nas khyod kyis rang gi dpa' ba bstan// de na rab tu dpung nyams re chad na// de ring ci phyir thams cad mkhyen la sngo// bdud ral gyi zla ba zhes
33b2(mdo sde): bya ba des 'di skad ces smras so// de ni su la yang yid kyis khro ba med// mi gnas de ni bsam pa nyid kyis gtsang // khams gsum dag las thar cing 'gro bar rgyu// de la gzhan
33b3(mdo sde): gyis bsad par mi nus so// sdig can gyis smras pa/ 'dod khams 'di na sems can gang 'khod pa/ 'dod la chags shing nga rgyal dregs pas myos// de dag daphyir rtag 'brang
33b4(mdo sde): phyag brnyan te// de dag tshogs pas ci phyir de ma sod// de nas bdud sa chu zhes bya ba des 'di skad ces smras so// snying po med cing sgyu ma smig rgyu 'dra// dngos po
33b5(mdo sde): kun shes sred pa rnam par btul// srid par mtshags na mkha'i ngo bo nyid// de la bgegs byed do/ nus par ga la 'gyur// sdig can gyis smras pa/ mi
33b6(mdo sde): yi 'jig rten 'di na de yang yod// bza' btung zhim po sman dang gos bstan cing // tshor ba gsum yang de y-i sems la yod// ci phyir de la brlag par bya bar nus// bdud sreg
33b7(mdo sde): spongs zhes bya ba des 'di skad ces smras so// sdig can lto 'phye chen po rnams kyi ni// rdzu 'phrul bdag cag yul ni ci yod pa// don 'grub 'phrul la cha shas mi reg na// de la
33b8(mdo sde): ji ltar brlag par bya bar nus// sdig can gyis smras pa/ ngas ni de la zan bcad byas// de la rdo ba dag kyang 'phangs// de bzhin mi snyan tshig smras nas// gnas dag nas kyang
34a1(mdo sde): rab tu bskyod// bdud shes mig ces bya ba des 'di skad ces smras so// khyod kyis gang tshe de la bgegs byas te// de ni khros pas cung zad tshig pa 'am/ 
34a2(mdo sde): khyod la khro gnyer bzhin yang bstan byos sam// de las khyod kyis tshig ngan mngon thos sam// sdig can gyis smras pa/ de ni so sor brtags pas rtag tu bzod// 'dod
34a3(mdo sde): chags spangs shing zhe sdang gti mug bral// de nas sems can kun la byams sems ldan// 'dre bar spyod pa yang de brtag go/ bdud thub dka' zhes bya ba des 'di skad ces
34a4(mdo sde): smras so// kun sbyor gsum gyi zhags pas gang bcing sa pa// de la bdag cag nan tan bgegs bya me nga // des ni skyon dang gti mug zhags pa spangs// 
34a5(mdo sde): la ji ltar brlags par bya bar nus// sdig can gyi// sa smras pa// stobs thob khyed cag nga'i grog/ sa yin te// khyed rnams bag yod byos la de'u re chos
34a6(mdo sde): thams cad phyogs su ri'i 'phreng ba dang // sa 'di ma lus byon gyis chur brlab bo// mkha' las mi bzad rtug pa'i zag char dang // lcags kyi phye ma'i phung po rab tu dbab/ 
34a7(mdo sde): lcags mda' mdung thung spu gri mda' bo che// de lus phye mar glag cing dbab par bya// kun nas rab tu rno ba'i ro rdo rje dang // mdung thung ral gri tho ba rnams pham la// 'bar ba
34a8(mdo sde): mngon 'phangs sbyor ba de dag gis// shAkya'i bu de thal bar glag par bya// de bzhin du bdud bya ba'i bar du thams cad kyis tshigs su bcad pa smras so// de nas bdud de dag thams
34b1(mdo sde): cad kyis/ mgrin gcig tu 'di skad ces smras so// de bzhin 'dong bar bgyi'o// rang rang gi gnas nas go 'gos la// sde dang g.yog tu bcas te 'dod ngo do// bdag cag gi rdzu 'phrul dang / 
34b2(mdo sde): stobs kyi yul de dag thams cad bstan par ni bya na dge sbyong go'u ta mde rtsal ci 'dra ba de'i mod la rab tu ston te/ khyod rang gis rig par 'gyur ro// de nas bdud bye ba rang gi gnas
34b3(mdo sde): su dong nas/ go bgos te bdud bye ba re re zhing yang g.yog stong stong ya yang rnam pa mang po gyon pa lag cha sna tshogs pa/ go rnam pa sna tshogs dgos pa dag dang chas te// de'i nub mo 'das

41a2(mdo sde): med pa yi// byang chub nam mkha'i rang bzhin reg par 'gyur// de lta bu'i don gyis tshig chos sgra de dag byung bas 'jig rten gyi khams 'dir mi dang / mi ma yin pa de dag tshogs te/ 
41a3(mdo sde): 'bad cing 'khod ngo // la la ni tshangs pa'i cha byad du/ la la ni dbang phyug gi cha byang du/ la la ni dbang phyug chen po'i cha byad du la la ni sred med kyi bu'i cha byad du/ la la ni
41a4(mdo sde): dga' ldan bI cha byad du/ la la ni 'thab bral ba'i cha byang du/ la la ni brgya byin gyi cha byang du/ la la da ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i cha byad du/ la la ni gzhon
41a5(mdo sde): nu'i cha byad du/ la la ni rnam thos kyi bu'i cha byad du/ la la ni 'phags skyes po'i cha byad du/ la la ni mig mi bzang gi cha byad du/ la la ni yul 'khor
41a6(mdo sde): srung gi cha byang du la la ni rgyal chen bzhi pa'i phal ba'i cha byad du/ la la ni nyi ma'i cha byad du la la ni zla ba'i cha byad du la la ni skar ma'i cha byad du/ la la ni
41a7(mdo sde): lha ma yin gyi cha byad du/ la la ni na mkha' lding gi cha byad du la la ni mi 'am ci'i cha byad du/ la la ni lto phye chen po'i cha byad du/ la la ni rin po che'i cha byad du/ la la
41a8(mdo sde): ni gser gyi rgyan gyi cha byad du/ la la ni rin po che sna tshogs kyi cha byad du la la ni rin po che'i shing ljon pa'i cha byad du/ la la ni rgyal rigs kyi cha byad du/ la la ni
41b1(mdo sde): gzhan mu stegs can gyi cha byang du/ la la ni 'khor lo rin po che'i cha byad du la la ni nor bu rin po che'i cha byad du/ la la ni glang po rin po che sa srung gi bu'i cha byad du/ 
41b2(mdo sde): la ni rta'i rgyal po sprin gyi shugs ldan gyi cha byad du la la ni bud med rin po che'i cha byad du/ la la ni tshong dpon btsun pa'i cha byad du/ la la ni blon po rin po che'i cha
41b3(mdo sde): byad du/ bdag nyid mngon par sprul te/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir 'khod do// la la ni sngo zhing kha dog sngo la// phyong 'phrul dang rgyan dkar pos brgyan par
41b4(mdo sde): bdag nyid mngon par sprul te/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir gdug pa dang / rgyal mtshan dadang / ba don dmar po dang / mu tig gi phreng ba thog
41b5(mdo sde): shing 'phang du ta la'i srid tsam gyi na mkha'i dkyil la/ khod do// la la ni dkar zhing kha dog dkar la/ phyang 'phrul dang / spud pa kha dog leb rgan te
41b6(mdo sde): gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan ser po dang / mu tig gi phreng ba thogs shing 'khod do// la la ni lab rgan kha dog leb rgan la gser gyi gos dang / phyang
41b7(mdo sde): phrul dang / lbab lhub ste/ rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan mthing ka thogs shing 'khod do// la la ni dmar zhing kha dog dmar la/ mu tig dmar po'i chang 'bebs so// 
41b8(mdo sde): la la ni dkar zhing kha dog dkar la mu tig dmar po'i char 'bebs so// la la ni lha'i drang song gi kha dog du bdag nyid mngon par sprul nas/ na mkha' las me tog gi char
42a1(mdo sde): mngon par 'bebs so// la la ni bcom ldan 'das kyi nyan thos kyi gzugs su mngon par sprul nas/ na mkha' las lha'i spos sna tshogs kyi char 'bebs so// 
42a2(mdo sde): la la ni dri zi'i kha dog gis lha'i sil snyan sna tshogs rdung ngo // la la ni lha'i bu mo'i kha dog gis rin po che sna tshogs kyi snod du spos chu thogs te/ sa la chag chag 'debs so// la
42a3(mdo sde): la ni mching bu nag po lta bu'i kha dog ste/ spos sna tshogs kyis rab tu bdug par byed do// la la ni lha'i bu'i cha byad kyis gar byed cing glu'i dbyangs 'byin to// la la ni kha dog sna tshogs
42a4(mdo sde): bcom ldan 'das ga la ba de logs su thal mo sbyar te/ bcom ldan 'das la bstod do// bdud dang bdud dkyi 'khor la la ni/ bcom ldan 'das phyogs ga la
42a5(mdo sde): bzhugs pa de logs su mngon par phyogs te/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir rin po tshe rnam pa sna tshogs thogs so// la la ni srang dang khang
42a6(mdo sde): pa dang / khyim dang / skar khung dang / rta babs dang / bsil khang dang / lam gyi bzhi mdo dang / sum mdo dang / khang po brtsegs pa dang / gzhal med khang rnams
42a7(mdo sde): na 'dug cing thal mo sbyar te/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir 'khod do// de nas bdud sdig can gyis gang gi tshe// bdud de dag thams cad g.yog dang bcas pa
42a8(mdo sde): dge sbyong go'u ta ma la skyabs su dong par mthong ba de'i tshe rab tu 'khrugs te/ skrag cing srang gi dbus na pad+ma de 'khor bar 'dug go// 'og min gyi lha grangs med dpag tu med
42b1(mdo sde): pa'i bar du 'og min nas babs nas chos mnyan pa'i phyir pad+ma de'i khor yug tu 'khod do// bdud sdig can gyis tshigs su bcad pa de dag thos nas kun tu bltas na/ rgyal po'i
42b2(mdo sde): khab kyi grong khyer chen po'i srang gi dbus na pad+ma de las 'di lta bu'i tshigs su bcad pa dag byung ste/ chos mnyan pa'i phyir mi bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med dpag tu
42b3(mdo sde): med pa dag gis pad+ma de 'khor bar 'khod par mthong ngo // de nas bdud sdig can gyis steng du bsdus na/ 'dod pa na spyod pa'i lha drug gi gnas thams cad na yang
42b4(mdo sde): chos mnyan pa'i phyir lnga bye ba phrag brgya stong grangs med dpag tu med pa dag gis pad+ma de dag 'khor bar 'khod par mthong ngo // de nas bdud sdig
42b5(mdo sde): can rab tu sdug bsngal zhing yid mi bde nas yod la bcags te/ spu zing zhes byed par gyur lus rdul te/ lus 'dar nas na mkha' la rgyug
42b6(mdo sde): cing skud chen bas bos te/ bdud gzhan la 'di skad ces smras so// mi 'gyur yid kyis d+ma'i tshig la nyon// nga la spobs med bdag yul 'dir dbang
42b7(mdo sde): thub stobs yon tan shin tu dri med de// skye bo bstan phyir 'jig rten 'dir 'jug go// lha mi dga' ba'i pad+ma 'dir byung ste// 'gro mchog ma lus nges par
42b8(mdo sde): nye bar dong // bder gshegs tshig la sgom zhing rab tu dgar// yon tan rab mchog zhi ba'i lam du 'gro// 'di ni 'jog rten gsum po srub dge sbyong rgya yin
43a1(mdo sde): te/ lha mi mang po thams cad yid gcig pad+ma 'khor bar 'jug/ da ni 'jigs pa'i skad phyung myur du ri'i char phab ste// ci nas bdud kyi sde chen mtshon
43a2(mdo sde): gyi sa dang bcom 'dir brlags kyis// de nas bdud gzhan zhig gis bdud sdig can la 'di skad ces smras so// bdag gi phan byed tshig 'di nyon cig khyod kyis chos rig na// 
43a3(mdo sde): bdag sde brlag pa mthong yang zhi bar ci'i phyir mi 'gro/ bder gshegs gzi brjid sku dang dpal gzugs mthong bas bdag cag myos// sangs rgyas 'dren pa ma gtogs
43a4(mdo sde): 'di na skyabs rab mchog gzhan med// de nas bdu dang gzhan zhig rab tu ngu zhing gdong mchog tu khros pas danon pas/ bdud sdig can la 'di skad ces smras so// 
43a5(mdo sde): log pa'i lam du zhugs shing lam dman pa// bad/ ga gi stobs mthu med pa'ang mi shes sam// 2 dran pa la yang gang phyir khyod sngo ba// ngo mi tsha 'am 'dzem pa
43a6(mdo sde): mi bya 'am// bdag cag stobs ni shin tu brlag par gyur// sangs rgyas mthu yis 'gro ba ma lus pa// pad ma'i drung du nye bar der dong ste// chos thos tshim pas lus kyang
43a7(mdo sde): shin tu dag/ bdag cag rnam par 'jigs shing skrag gyur te// lus ni dra nga stobs dang brtson 'grus stor// ji tsam skad cig brlag par ma gyur pa// de'i bar du
43a8(mdo sde): thub dbang skyabs su 'dong // de nas bdud gzhan zhig gis thal mo sbyar te/ 'di skad ces smras so// sdig can khyod ni chos kyi spyod pa spangs shing sdig byed dga'/ 
43b1(mdo sde): sangs rgyas mgon 'di 'gro ba'i phan don mkhas shing dge ba'i mchog/ grong khyer 'dir byon bdag cag myur du dga' zhing dang bas blta// 'jig rten gsum mchod srog
43b2(mdo sde): chags kun gyi sman la skyabs su 'dong // de nas na mkha' nyid nas bdud dbyangs kyi blo gros shes bya ba des sgra chen por 'di skad ces smras so// khyed kun tshogs pas gus
43b3(mdo sde): shing dga' ldan pa'i tshig nyon// sdig pa'i lta ba kun bzlog lus btung yad 'thun spyod pa de// khro spangs rab dga' thub pa'i gsung mchog la yong dga' dang bskyed// 
43b4(mdo sde): sangs rgyas mngon sum rnyed dka' skyabs de de ring gu das par mchod// de nas skad cig de nyid la bdud thams cad na mkha' las babs nas rgyal po'i khab
43b5(mdo sde): kyi grong khyer gyi sgo rin po che sna bdun las byas te/ bdud la la ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'o/ byang du bdag nyid mngon sprul nas/ bcom ldan 'ad
43b6(mdo sde): la mchod pa'i phyir 'bad cing 'khod do// la la ni tshangs pa'i cha byang du// la ni dbang byed kyi cha byad du/ la la ni dbang phyug chen po'i cha byad du/ la la ni sred med
43b7(mdo sde): kyi bu'i cha byad du/ la la ni dga' ldan pa'i cha byad du/ la la ni 'thab bral ba'i cha byad du/ la la ni brgya byin gyi cha byad du/ la la ni sum cu rtsa gsum pa'i cha byad du/ 
43b8(mdo sde): la la ni gzhon nu'i cha byad du/ la la ni rnam thos kyi bu'i cha byad du/ la la ni 'phags skyes po'i cha byad du// la la ni mig mi bzang gi cha byad du la la ni yul 'a'o/ 
44a1(mdo sde): bsrung gim byung du/ la la ni rgyal chem mal pa'i cha byad du/ lal ni nyi ma'i cha byad du/ lal ni rdza ba na byad du/ lal ni m+b+ha ma
44a2(mdo sde): cha byad du/ la la ni lha ma yin gyi cha byad du/ la la ni na mkha' lding gi cha byad du/ la la ni mi'am ci'i cha byad du/ la la ni lto 'phye chen po'i cha byad du/ la la ni rin po che'i
44a3(mdo sde): cha byad du/ la la ni gser gyi rgyan gyi cha byad du/ la la ni rin po che sna tshogs kyi cha byad du/ la la ni rin po che'i shing ljon pa'i cha byad du/ la la ni rgyal rigs kyi cha byad du/ 
44a4(mdo sde): la la ni gzhan mu stegs can gyi cha byad du/ la la ni 'khor lo rin po che'i cha byad du/ la la ni nor dbu rin po che'i cha byad du/ la la ni glang po ches srung gi
44a5(mdo sde): bu'i cha byad du/ la la ni rta'i rgyal po sprin gyi shug can gyi cha byad du la la ni bud med rin po che'i chabyad du la la ni tshong dpon btsun pa'i cha byad du
44a6(mdo sde): la la ni blon po rin po che'i cha byad du/ bdag nyid mngon par sprul te/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir 'khod do// la la ni sngo zhing kha dog sngo la byang phrul dang
44a7(mdo sde): rgyan dkar pos brgyan par bdag nyid mngon par sprul te/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir/ gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dmar po dang / mu

44b1(mdo sde): gdugs dang rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan ser po dang / mu tig gi phreng ba thogs shing 'khod// la la ni leb rgan ladog le ba rgan la gser gyi gos dang byung

44b3(mdo sde): char 'bebs so// la la ni dkar zhing kha dog dkar la/ mu tig dmar po'i char 'bebs so// la la ni lha'i drang srong gi kha dog tu bdag nyid mngon par sprul nas/ na mkha'

44b5(mdo sde): 'bebs so// la la ni dri za'i kha dog gis lha'i sil snyan sna tshogs rdung ngo // la la ni lha'i bu mo'i kha dog sa rin po che sna tshogs kyi snod du/ spos chu thogs

45a1(mdo sde): la la ni srang dang / khang pa dang / skar khung dang / rta babs dang / bsil khang dang / lam gyi bzhi mdo dang / sum mdo dang / khang pa brtsegs padang

45a3(mdo sde): g.yog dang bcas te/ dge sbyong go'u ta ma la skyabs su dong bar mthong ba de'i tshe/ rab tu 'khrugs te skrag cing myos nas rab tu ngu zhing 'di skad ces smras so// phyin chad grogs med de/

45a6(mdo sde): babs te/ srang gi pad+ma ga la der phyin nas/ pad+ma de'i sdong po yan chad dbyung bar 'dod na/ reg par yang ma nus/ pad+ma'i 'dab ma bcad par 'dod na/ de dag kyang ma
45a7(mdo sde): mthong / pad+ma'i snying po la lag pas brdab par 'dod na de yang mi dmigs te/ dper na glog snang yang mi dmigs pa bzhin no// 'di lta ste/ dper na/ grib ma snang yang mi dmigs
45a8(mdo sde): pa de bzhin du pad+ma de yang snang mod kyi mi dmigs so// gang gi tshe bdud sdig can gyis pad+ma de mthong yang mi dmigs shing reg par mi rung ba de'i tshe/ 'khor thams cad rab tu
45b1(mdo sde): spangs par bya ba'i phyir skad drag cing che la 'jigs pa'i sgra dbyung bar 'dod na de yang ma nus so// yang stobs chen po'i drag shul gyis lag pa gnyis sa chen po la brdabs te
45b2(mdo sde): rab tu bskyod par 'dod na/ reg par yang ma nus te mi dmigs so// 'di lta ste/ dper na/ la la zhig na mkha' la rdob par 'dod na mi dmigs pa de bzhin du/ bdud
45b3(mdo sde): sdig can gyis sa mthong yang reg par mi rung zhing mi dmigs nas/ de 'di snyam du sems te/ ci nas sems can 'dus pa rnams brtags te/ sems rnam par 'khrugs par bya'o//

45b7(mdo sde): bdag gi gnas su 'gro bar 'dod na der yang 'gro bar ma nus te// de rab tu skrag cing ngus nas 'di snyam du sems so// bdag gi rdzu 'phrul gyi stobs zad de/ bdag dge sbyong

46a1(mdo sde): can gcig gis kyang bdag 'chi ba'i dus byed pa mi mthong bar sangs rgyas kyi zhing mi mjed kyi pha rol tu 'chi ba'i dus bya'o snyam na/ 'od kyang mi snang bar bya ba 'am/ 
46a2(mdo sde): phyogs dang phyogs mtshams su 'bros kyang ma nus te/ de nyid du mgul pa bcing ba lngas bcings par bdag gis mthong bar rab tu khros shing skrag ste/ skad chen por ngu zhing 'di

47a1(mdo sde): nam mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po brgya stong mang po bcom ldan 'das kyi snyan pa la dad pa rnams gdong mchi ma can gyis 'di skad ces smras so// 
47a2(mdo sde): chos kyi kha lo sgyur mchog mya ngan med bzhugs kyang // rgyal ba'i bstan pa 'di lta bu yi gnas gyur te// nyan thos de dag la ni rgyal ka dang byas pa// 'gro ba rnams kyis mthong / 
47a3(mdo sde): na dad par ga la 'gyur// de nas lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / na mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / srin po bye
47a4(mdo sde): ba khrag khrig mang po gdong mchi ma can gyis bcom lda ngan 'das ga la ba der lhags te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar 'khod nas/ 'di skad ces gsol to//

60b3(mdo sde): ldan 'das kyi zhabs gnyis la gtugs ma thag tu de nas thams cad dang ldan pa'i stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di rnam pa drug tu g.yos//

60b5(mdo sde): to/ gang dag glang po ches 'dul ba'i sems can/ de dag gis ni/ bde bar gshegs pa glang/ po che'i gzugs su mthong nas yid dga' bar
60b6(mdo sde): gyur cing / drang srong chen po skar ma la dga' bas me tog gtor ba de dag steng gi bar snang la gdugs su gyur to// gnas pa dang / sa g.yos pa de yang mtho
60b7(mdo sde): nas rab tu ngo mtshar du gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs gnyis la gtugs so// gang dag yang sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i sems can de dag thams cad/ 
60b8(mdo sde): kyis ni/ bcom ldan 'das sangs rgyas kyi cha byad du mthong nas ngo mtshar du gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das dpa' bar 'gro ba'i ting nge 'dzin las bzhengs
61a1(mdo sde): pa dang / sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i sems can de dag gis ting nge 'dzin de la bzhengs par mthong nas/ zang zing med cing mchog tu dga' bad
61a2(mdo sde): mgu ba skyes te/ bcom ldan 'das la me tog dang / spos dang / phreng ba dang / byug pa dang / na bza' dang / byang phrul dang / rgyan ji snyed pa de dag gis gtor to// 
61a3(mdo sde): de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag bka' stsal to// drang srong chen po myur du longs la nyon// byang chub lung bstan zhes ni 'dren pa gsung / 
61a4(mdo sde): mnyam pa med pa'i mthus ni sa g.yos shing // na mkha' la yang me tog gtugs gcig 'dug// khyod ni 'jig rten phan phyir ston dang dbang po// rkang gnyis
61a5(mdo sde): dag gi gtso bo sangs rgyas su// bsod nams mtha' yas na mkha' tshad mnyam pa// khams gsum snying por 'gro ba'i sgron mar 'gyur// de nas byang
61a6(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po skar ma la dga' bas// bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// gang du bdag chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar 'gyur ba'i
61a7(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi zhing de ci 'dra bar 'gyur/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ khyod ni bskal pa grangs med dpag tu med pa na// byang phyogs su sangs rgyas kyi zhing
61a8(mdo sde): me tog rgyas pa'i dri zhes bya ba 'byung ste/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing de ni ji ltar da ltar gyi 'jig rten gyi khams bde ba can bzhin du bkod pa de lta bu dang ldan par 'gyuraro// sangs
61b1(mdo sde): rgyas kyi zhing der skyes bu dam pa khyod bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
61b2(mdo sde): pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs pa 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ skyes bu 'dul ba'i kha lo sgyur ba/ bla na med pa/ lha dang mi rnams kyi ston pa
61b3(mdo sde): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rdul med spos snang skar ma'i dpal zhes bya bar gyur te/ khyod kyi tshe'i tshad ni bar gyi bskal pa bcu thub par 'gyuraro// sangs rgyas kyi zhing de na
61b4(mdo sde): nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas med cing / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po 'ba' shig gi gnas su 'gyur te/ khyod kyang de na theg pa chen
61b5(mdo sde): po'i gtam 'ba' shig ston par 'gyuraro// 'khor ji snyed lhags pa rnams kyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po skar ma la dga' ba'i
61b6(mdo sde): lung bstan pa de thos nas/ bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa'i las byed pa la brtson par gyur to// bram ze'i khye'u lnga brgya po de dag dang / srog chags bye ba khrag
61b7(mdo sde): khrig brgya stong phrag dgu bcu rtsa gnyis kyis/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed par gyur te/ de dag thams cad kyis/ byang chub sem
61b8(mdo sde): dpa'i tong nge 'dzin byang chub kyi sems mi brjed pa zhes bya ba thob bo// 'dus pa chen po rin po che tog gi gzungs las drang srong skar ma la dga' ba'i le'u ste bzhi pa'o// / 
62a1(mdo sde): de nas bdud bye bdag 'di snyam du sems te/ ji ltar grong khyer 'dar phyi rol lha dang / klu da nga gnod sbyin dag gis brgyan pa de bzhin du/ bdag cag
62a2(mdo sde): gis kyang bcom ldan 'das grong khyer 'di'i sgo gang nas gshegs pa'i de'i sgo dang de'i sa phyogs bkod pa'i rgyan bkod dam pa khyad par du 'phags pas brgyan to snyam pa dang
62a3(mdo sde): de nas bcom ldan 'das kyi thugs kyis bdud bye ba de dag gi sems kyi kun tu rtog pa mkhyen nas/ 'di 'dra ba'i rdzu 'phrul mngon par 'du bya ba mngon par mdzad do// 
62a4(mdo sde): de ji lta bu'i rdzu 'phrul mngon par 'du bya ba mngon par 'du mdzad pas/ grong khyer gyi sgo bcuganyis su sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das bcu gnyis grong khye
62a5(mdo sde): gyi sgo re re nas/ rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer chen por gshegs so// bdud bye ba de dag kyang na mkha 'a la gnas bzhin du bdud kyi yul gyi rnam par 'phrul
62a6(mdo sde): pa'i rgyan shin tu khyad par du 'phags pa rdzu 'phrul grangs med pa dang ldan pa/ bkod pa'i mchog rnams dang / dkod pa mdzes pa rnams kyis grong khyer gyi sgo de dag dang / 
62a7(mdo sde): sa'i phyogs de dag dang / rtsig pa de dag dang / shing de dag dang / sa'i ngos de dag brgyan to// bdud bye ba de dag dang / bdud kyi 'khor de dag la la dag ni/ tshangs
62a8(mdo sde): pa'i cha byad lta bu nas drang srong chen po'i cha byad lta bu'i bar du bsgyur te/ na mkha' la gnas bzhin du khang pa brtsegs pa de dag gi skar khung dang / rta babs dang / bag ma
62b1(mdo sde): dang / skyed shing gi nang na me tog dang / spyos dang / bdug pa dang / phreng ba dang / gser dang / dngul dang / nor bu dang / mu tig sna tshogs kyis spras pa dang /

62b3(mdo sde): yon tan bsngags pa sna tshogs kyi dbyangs kyis// bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa byed do// bcom ldan 'das de ltar ngo mtshar rmad du byung ba chen po sngon ma thos pa'i bkod
62b4(mdo sde): pa mchog tu rgya che ba khyed par du 'bogs pas/ rgyal dpo'i khab kyi grong khyer chen po'i sgron bzhugs te// zhabs g.yas pa'i mthe bos sgo'i them pa la reg par

62b6(mdo sde): rten gyi khams 'di rab tu g.yos so// gang stong gsum gyi stong chen po'i 'jig rten gyi khams 'di brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / nyi ma dang / zla ba dang / 'jig
62b7(mdo sde): rten skyong ba dang / dbang phyug chen po dang / lha dang klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / na mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen

63a1(mdo sde): lha'i drang srong chen po'i 'khor dang / 'og min gyi bar nas bzung ste/ sems can gzi brjid che ba gzi brjid che ba de dag thams cad sa g.yos par
63a2(mdo sde): snang ba des bskul ma thag tu rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer chen po kho ra khor yug tu bskor nas/ sa dang na mkha' la gnas shing / me tog dang / spos dus kyi rjes su 'brang
63a3(mdo sde): ba'i phye ma'i bar gyis/ bcom ldan 'das la gtor to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis me tog dang / phye ma'i bar de dag phyogs bcu'i phyogs cha re re na yang
63a4(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi zhing rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed kyi sangs rgya ngas kyi zhing yongs su dag pa dang / yongs su ma dag/ pa dang / stong pa dang / mi stong pa rnams su sangs
63a5(mdo sde): rgyas la mchod cing ste stang bya ba'i phyir na mkha' la btor ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag tu ma dang / phye ma dang / rgyan de dag las tshig su
63a6(mdo sde): bcad pa 'di dag byung ngo // myur du sad par gyis la 'di dag ltos// byang chub phyir ni bag yod spyad pa spyod// khyod kyis 'khor ba'i gcong rong 'khyam pa yi//

63b1(mdo sde): ba rang gis pham mdzad des// da ni chos kyi 'khor lo myur du bskor// grogs po zhi ba 'di la 'gro dga' mdzad// dpa' mchog dngos po yang dag ston pa mdzad// 'gro
63b2(mdo sde): ba'i sdug bsngal dag las thar mdzad nas// byang chub tu ni de ring lung yang ston// rang byung mya ngan med pa'i grong khyer gshegs// de phyir zhing der rab tu myur shegs la// / 
63b3(mdo sde): de ltar mdzes pa de dag rab ltos te// rim gyis byang chub tu yang 'gyur bar byos// yang de'i tshe 'od ma'i tshal na byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dang / nyan thos
63b4(mdo sde): dang / nyan thos chen po gang dag nang du yang dag 'jog la gnas pa de dag gis ston pa de la bltas pa dang / bcom ldan 'das rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer chen por

63b6(mdo sde): kyi snam logs su 'khod pa dang / bkod pa chen po de dag kyang mthong ngo // de nas me tog dang / phye ma'i rgyan de dag las tshigs su bcad pa'i sgra gang yin pa de dag gis

64a1(mdo sde): du sems te/ yid du 'ong ba 'di lta bu ro myang bar 'os pa 'di lta bu/ dga' bar bya bar 'os pa 'di lta bu tshim par byed pa 'di lta bu/ spro bar
64a2(mdo sde): byed pa 'di lta bu/ yon tan chen po brjod par 'os pa 'di lta bu'i sgo 'di dang / me tog dang / bye ma'i char 'di yang ga las 'ongs sam mo// de nas byang chub sems
64a3(mdo sde): dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag dang / nyan thos chen po de dag rang gi dge ba'i phyogs btang ste/ ngo mtshar cher 'dzin par gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das
64a4(mdo sde): de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rgyan dang / lhab lhub kyi rgyu 'thun pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so//

64a6(mdo sde): dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed 'di dang phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du bkod pa chen po 'di lta bu 'di snang ste/ 'di lta ste/ ma 'ongs
64a7(mdo sde): pa'i dus na/ de bzhin gshegs pa kun tu gzigs shes bya ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams rnam par dag cing // rdul bsags pa med ces bya ba yang sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi
64a8(mdo sde): yon tan bkod pa 'di 'dra ba dang ldan par 'gyur/ rtsig pa med pa la legs par rgyan pa'i phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul phra rab kyi
64b1(mdo sde): rdul snyed thams cad du yang bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa de rgyal po'i khab kyi grong khyer chen po'i sgo nas shin tu lham me/ lhan ne/ lhang nger bzhugs
64b2(mdo sde): par snang ba ni ma gtogs so// sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag tu yang byang chub sems dpa' de dag dang / nyan thos chen po de dag sgra thos pa des bskul ba dang / phyogs
64b3(mdo sde): bzhir lta zhing 'khod de/ de dag thams cad kyis 'jig rten gyi khams mo mjed 'di/ ha cang yang mi ring ba na 'dug par mthong ngo // sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis

64b5(mdo sde): de dag 'di snyam du sems te/ bdag cag kyang 'du sa pa chen po'i bkod pa de dag dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi yon tan bkod pa de dag blta ba dang
64b6(mdo sde): brtag pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa de la blta ba dang / phyag bya ba dang / bsnyen bkur bya ba'i phyir der 'dong ngo // der ni bdag cag bla na med
64b7(mdo sde): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lung bstan pa yang thob par 'gyur gor ma chag snyam mo// de nas phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing rdul phra ra
64b8(mdo sde): snyed thams cad kyi/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dang / nyan thos chen po de dag de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa'i rdzu 'phrul gyi mthus// rang rang gi sangs
65a1(mdo sde): rgyas kyi zhing nas mi snang bar gyur te/ skad cig thang cig yud tsam de nyid la 'jig rten gyi khams mi mjed 'dir byin to// de'i tshe phyogs bcu
65a2(mdo sde): phyogs re re nas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po grangs med dpag tu med pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing rdul phra rab kyi rdul snyed rnams kyang 'dir lhags nas

65b1(mdo sde): dang ras dang / ras bcos ma sna tshogs kyi char rab tu phab po// bcom ldan 'das la mchod pa bya ba'i phyir/ la la dag gis ni rin po che'i gdugs dang / rgya la maH/

80a4(mdo sde): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang / phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ba dang / lung bstan pa thob par gyur cig/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'ad
80a5(mdo sde): de dag thams cad kyis kyang / chos bstan pa'i phyir cang mi gsung bar gyur pas/ gnang nas pad+ma'i snying po de dag la bzhugs so// ji ltar sangs rgyas kyi
80a6(mdo sde): zhing thams cad du gtogs pa'i sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal thams cad zhi bar 'gyur ba dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad bsngags pa'i phyir dran pa dang / dad pa dang / 
80a7(mdo sde): dang ba dang / mos pa rnyed par 'gyur ba dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mthong ma thag tu sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'dir gtogs pa'i sems can rnams kyi sems dang / 
80a8(mdo sde): sems las byung ba rnams la 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug dang / lta ba ngan pa dang / nga rgyal dang / rgyags pa dang / dregs pa dang / 'jig tshogs la lta ba dang / 
80b1(mdo sde): the tshom dang / nye bar len pa dang / srid pa'i sred pa kun gzhi'i nyes pa dag rab tu zhi bar 'gyur ba dang / sems can so so nas 'di snyam du bdag cag gcig pu de bzhin
80b2(mdo sde): gshegs pa'i spyan snga na chos nyan pa'i phyir 'dug gi/ 'di na gzhan ni su yang med do// bdag cag cig pu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs thams cad kyis dgongs te// 
80b3(mdo sde): nad thams cad rab tu zhi bar bya ba'i phyir chos ston par bzhed do// 'di na bzhin sus kyang de bzhin gshegs pa la chos mnyan pa'i phyir gsol ba ma btab po snyam du shes
80b4(mdo sde): par 'gyur ba de lta bu'i sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi smon de lam mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pa'i ting nge 'dzin la snyom par zhugs so// yang de'i tshe gang sangs rgyas kyi
80b5(mdo sde): zhing ma lus pa 'dir gtogs pa'i sems can rnams dbang po thams cad bstan te/ thal mo sbyar nas/ de dag gis mgrin gcig tu 'di skad ces gsol to// 
80b6(mdo sde): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis bdag cag la chos bshad du gsol/ btsun pa bde bar gshegs pa rnams kyis bdag cag la bshad du gsol/ bdag gis
80b7(mdo sde): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos nan tan gyis bsdu bar bgyi'o// de nas yang de'i tshe de bzhin gshegs pa shAkya thub pa des sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
80b8(mdo sde): gzhan rnams la mchod pa'i phyir spos bkod pa las shin tu lhag pa'i spos gong du mchog tu khyad par du gyur pa/ rgya chen pos sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di thams cad khyab
81a1(mdo sde): par byin gyis rlabs so// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das lhag ma rnams mchod pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du gtogs pa'i sems can thams cad kyi
81a2(mdo sde): lag na rin po che dang / me tog dang / phreng ba dang / spos dang / byug pa sna tshogs dang / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / rgyan dang / lhab lhub sna tshogs dag gis gang
81a3(mdo sde): bar byin gyis brlabs nas 'di skad ces gsung ngo // da ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das gang ji snyed phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan dang / gzhan dag nas bdag gi sangs
81a4(mdo sde): rgyas kyi zhing du dri ba'i phyir byon pa rnams dgongs su gsol// / bdag sngon gyi smon lam gyis 'di 'dra bar rab tu nyon mongs pa can snyigs ma lnga dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten du/ 
81a5(mdo sde): bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par/ rdzogs par sangs rgyas te/ sems can bsam pa nyams pa lam rab tu stor ba/ ma rig pa'i mun pa dang / 
81a6(mdo sde): rab rib kyi ling tog gis nyon mongs pa'i mun par bcug pa/ ngan song gsum du zhugs pa/ mi dge ba dang 'grogs pa/ dge ba thams cad dang bral ba/ thabs mkhas pa thams
81a7(mdo sde): cad kyis yongasu spangs pa/ mtshams med pa byed pa/ dam pa'i chos spong ba/ 'phags pa la bskur pa 'debs pa/ snying rje med pa'i bsam pa can gyi sems can rnams la
81a8(mdo sde): snying rje ba'i slad du/ snying brtse ba dang / brtson 'grus kyi stobs kyi brtson pa chen pos grang ba dang / gro ba dang / rlung dang / tsha ba dang / ngal ba dang / chad pa dang du blang bar
81b1(mdo sde): bgyi'o// grong dang grong khyer dang / grong rdal dang / ljongs dang / yul dang / yul 'khor du rkang gis 'gro bar bgyi'o// sems can la phan par bgyi ba'i slad du/ rtsub pa dang /

81b3(mdo sde): dang / gso ma'i ras dang / phyag dar khrod gyi gos bgo bar bgyi'o// ri dang ro'i sul dang / nags stug po dang / grong stong pa dang / dur khrod du gnas par bgyi ba nas/ rtsa'i
81b4(mdo sde): mal cha dang / gso ma dang / shing gi 'dab ma/ rtsub pa// dri mi zhim pa reg na mi bde ba'i mal tshe spyad par bgyi'o// bdag gis thabs mkhas pa dang / snying rje chen
81b5(mdo sde): po dang / brtson 'grus kyi go cha bgos nas/ sems can rnams la gtam rnam pa sna tshogs bgyis/ te/ rgyal rigs rnams la ni rgyal srid dang dbang phyug gi
81b6(mdo sde): gtam bgyi'o// bram ze rnams la ni rig byed dang / skar ma'i gtam dang / blon po rnams la ni yul dang las kyi mtha'i gtam dang / sman pa rnams la ni khams dang / 
81b7(mdo sde): sman dang / bsgrub pa'i gtam dang / tshong pa rnams la ni nyo tshong gi gtam dang / dmangs rnams la ni las kyi mtha' la mngon par zhen pa'i gtam dang / bud med rnams la
81b8(mdo sde): ni/ kha dog dang / rgyan dang / bu dang / byug pa dang / 'gran zla med pa'i gtam dang / dge sbyong rnams la bzod pa dang / nges pa dang / las gsum la rtson pa'i gtam bgyi'o// / 
82a1(mdo sde): sems can yongasu smin par bgyi ba'i spyad du/ ma thob pa thob par bgyi ba dang / mngon sum du ma bgyis pa mngon du bgyi bar gzung ngo do// mthar pa rnams
82a2(mdo sde): rab tu thar par bgyi ba'i slad du/ sdug bsngal rnam pa sna tshogs la spro bar bgyi'o// sems can yongasu smin par bgyi ba'i slad du/ yul rgyu bar bgyi'o// de lta mod kyi sem
82a3(mdo sde): can 'di dag ni de na bdag bdag la gshe'o// mi snyan pa zer ro// phra dog gi chos kyi rgyus bdag la 'khrog pa'i kyis med pa la skur pa 'debs so// kha gsag dang / tshul
82a4(mdo sde): 'chos dang / rgyu dang / g.yo dang / brdzun smra ba dang / zhe gcod pa dang / bud med kyi tshig dag gis skur pa 'debs so// bdag la sas 'thor ro// bdag gsad
82a5(mdo sde): pa'i phyir mtshon dang / dug dang / me dang / 'khor lo dang mda' bo che dang / mda' dang / ral gri dang / ma dung dang / dgra sta dang / rdo dang / mtshon cha'i char 'bebs/

82a7(mdo sde): bdag gi gnas dang / gnas khang dang / gtsug lag khang yang mi gtsang ba dang / dri nga bas 'gengs so// bdag gi nyan thos grong khyer du zhugs pa rnams la/ 'phags pa
82a8(mdo sde): ma yin pa'i sems can rnams kyis glu dang / gar tshul ma yin pa byed du btsud do// thabs brgya stong du mas bdag gsad pa'i phyir brtson no// bdag gi bstan pa nub par
82b1(mdo sde): bya ba dang / chos kyi tshul gyi sgron ma bsad pa dang / chos kyi rgyal mtshan brtul ba dang / chos kyi gru gzhig pa dang / bdag gi chos kyi mchod sbyin rnam par gtor ba'i phyir/ 
82b2(mdo sde): brtson no// da sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gi chos kyi tshul la gzigs te/ ji ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag
82b3(mdo sde): gis sangs rgyas kyi zhing nyon mongs pa can snyigs ma lnga dang ldan pa 'dir/ 'dus pa chen po mdzad nas/ dam pa'i chos kyi tshul yun ring du gnas par bgyi ba dang / bdud kyi
82b4(mdo sde): stobs kyi yul thams cad rab tu gzhom pa dang / dkon mchog gsum gyi rigs gnas pa rgyun mi 'chad par bgyi ba dang // sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa
82b5(mdo sde): ba 'phel bar bgyi ba dang dgra dang / phas kyi rgol ba/ thams cad chos dang 'thun pas tshar bcad pa/ dang / sems can rnams kyi 'thab pa dang / rtsod pa
82b6(mdo sde): dang rnga mu ge dang / nad dang / phas kyi dmag tshogs dang / 'ching ba dang / 'gyed pa dang / rgol ba dang / dus ma yin par grang ba dang / tsha ba dang / char dang / rlung dang /

82b8(mdo sde): thams cad 'dun par bgyi ba dang / khyim dang / grong dang / grong khyer dang / grong rdal dang / yul 'khor thams cad bsdus pa dang / g.yo dang / dug dang / byang dang / 
83a1(mdo sde): rmongs byed dang / rmi lam ngan pa dang / ltas ngan pa thams cad gzhil ba dang / 'bru dang / sman dang / me tog dang / 'bras bu dang / bcud thams cad kyis
83a2(mdo sde): sems can nye bar 'tsho bar bgyi ba dang / rgyal rigs dang / bram ze dang / dmangs rigs dang / rje'u rigs rnams dge ba spyod pa la gzung ba dang / byang chub kyi sems rab tu
83a3(mdo sde): bskyed pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa rnams la gzud pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams thabs shes pa la mkhas pa dang / dran pa dang / blo gros dang / 
83a4(mdo sde): rtogs pa dang / mos pa dang / dpa' ba dang / brtan pa dang / spobs pa rnam par 'phel bar bgyi/ da ba dang / dbang bskur ba'i sar dbugs dbyung ba la 'dzud
83a5(mdo sde): cing ye shes kyi pha rol tu 'gro bar bgyi ba'i slad du/ sngon gyi de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas de dag gis chos mnyam
83a6(mdo sde): pa nyid rdo rje lta bu brten pa'i chos kyi snying pos lus 'jom pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs phyag rgya dang / tshig rab tu dbye ba la 'jug pa lung bstan pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di bshad cing
83a7(mdo sde): byin gyis brlabs so// gcig la gcig dgyes pa des 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das da ltar phyogs bcu na bzhugs shing gzhes pa dag/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing snyis
83a8(mdo sde): ma lnga dang ldan pa 'dir dri ba'i phyir/ gshegs te bzhugs pa de dag thams cad kyis sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di bsrung ba'i slad du chos mnyam pa nyid rdo rje lta bu brten pa'i chos
83b1(mdo sde): kyi snying pos lus 'joms pa zhes bgyi ba'i gdungs phyag rgya dang / tshig rab tu dbye ba la 'jug pa lung bstan pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di dam pa'i chos kyi tshul yun ring du
83b2(mdo sde): gnas par bgyi ba dang / bdud kyi yul gyi stobs thams cad rab tu gzhom pa dang / ji ltar gong du rgyas par brjod pa bzhin du sgrib pa med pa'i ye shes kyi pha rol tu 'grib
83b3(mdo sde): bgyi ba'i bar gyi slad du/ bdag gis gsol ba btab pa la thugs brtse bar mdzad de/ gang sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'dir dam pa'i chos kyi tshul yun ring du gnas shing pas kyi rgol
83b4(mdo sde): ba thams cad kyis mi tshugs pa dang / mi 'jig das pa'i chos can du gyur pa dang / dkon mchog ga dasum gyi rigs mi 'chad pa dang / chos kyi sems can thams
83b5(mdo sde): cad nye bar 'tsho bar bgyi ba'i slad du legs par bshad du gsol/ byin gyis rlabs tu gsol/ bshad nas kyang phan tshun rjes su dgyes pa mdzad du gsol/ 
83b6(mdo sde): de nas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag gis 'di skad ces gsungs so// de bzhin du bdag cag gis sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'dir sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa la lag skyong bgyi
83b7(mdo sde): steng/ chos kyi tshul yun ring du gnas pa dang / bdud kyi yul gyi stobs thams cad rab tu gzhom pa nas sgrib pa med pa'i ye shes kyi pha rol tu 'gro bar bgyi ba'i bar gyi slad
83b8(mdo sde): du byin gyis rlabs cing chos mnyam pa nyid rdo rje lta bu brten pa'i chos kyi snying pos lus 'jom pa zhes bgyi ba'i gzungs phyag rgya dang tshigs rab tu dbye ba la 'jug pa lung bstan pa
84a1(mdo sde): chos kyi rnam grangs 'di bshad kyis gang su dag sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'dir gtogs pa'i sems can thams cad nyon cig// 'di lta ste/ A gar/ 
84a2(mdo sde): a ga ra/ bang gA ra/ pra bang ka ra/ b+ha ya mi hA/ mi tra ma b+hA se/ a khaM a kha/ a ma bA re/ do me/ do mad te/ ke bad de/ ke sU raM/ sa ma bA ha ne/ sa man ta b+hatwe/ d+harme/ d+haH/

85b1(mdo sde): skye mched drug yongasu sbyang bar bya ba nas/ sems can thams cad bla na med pa'i mya ngan las 'das pa thob par bya ba'i bar gyi phyir da ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das tham

85b3(mdo sde): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po gang ga'i klung suM cu rtsa drug gi bye ma snyed dag/ gzungs mngon par bsgrubs pa'i ting nge 'dzin dang / bzod pa thob par gyur to// yang de'i tshe/

85b6(mdo sde): zhugs che// mkhas pa 'di ni rnyed par dka'// gang 'di thugs rje ldan pa yi// mgon pos chos tshul byin brlabs pas// phyag rgya 'di 'dra thos pa yang // mchog tu rnyed par
85b7(mdo sde): dka' ba'o// bdud kyi phyogs rnams thams cad dang // dgra rnams kyang ni pham byed pa// dkon mchog gsum rgyun mi 'chad pa// rdzogs sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs/ 
85b8(mdo sde): bsgrib pa thams cad bsal ba'i phyir// bzod dang des pa rab 'phel ba// sems can rnams kyang 'dun byed pa// rgyal po dang ni yul 'khor skyong // 'din ngan byas zlog
86a1(mdo sde): byed pa// lta ba ngan pa rab 'gog pa// byang chub sems dpa' dbugs 'byin pa// byang chub lam yang rab ston pa// pha rol phyin pa 'phel byed pa// bzang po
86a2(mdo sde): spyod pa rdzogs byed pa// thabs dang ye shes spobs pa rnams// 'phel bar bya phyir byin gyis brlabs// dkar po'i phyogs ni sdud byed pa// gzungs ni gzhan gyis mi thub pa//

92b3(mdo sde): ci'ang ma yin pa cha shas med pa/ dngos po thams cad spangs pa/ de bzhin du rigs kyi bu sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams de bzhin nyid kyi phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams ni yang
92b4(mdo sde): dag pa'i mtha' yongasu bcad pa'o// bri ba med pa dang / gang ba med pa'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams ni pha rol dang tshu rol la reg pa med pa'o// cha shas
92b5(mdo sde): med pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams ni brjod du/ med pa'o// mau g.yo zhing rnam par gzhag pa ma da pa'i phyir sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams ni rdzas dang /

93a1(mdo sde): de ci'i slad du ye shes dang / brtson 'grus dang / thabs dang pha rol gnon pas khyod 'di ltar bdag la 'tshe/ bdag gi bdud kyi yul 'jom/ bdag gi

93a7(mdo sde): nad mi bzad pas btab ste/ sdug bsngal gyi tshor ba myong zhing lus kyang rul la dri nga bar gyur pa de 'dra ba'i gsang sngags kyi tshig rnams bshad/ yang de'i tshe/ bdud drug

94a3(mdo sde): cag gis kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed par bgyi na/ ji ltar bdag cag sangs rgyas kyi chos na mkha'i rang bzhin lta bu de dag man

94b1(mdo sde): bdag gis dbyung bar bgyi'o// gang du byung ba der ni shin tu lhag par bgyi'o// grong dang grong khyer dang / grong rdal dang / yul de dag na rigs kyi bu dang rigs kyi bu mo gang

95a1(mdo sde): na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar yang mi 'gyur bas/ bcom ldan 'das bdag der mchis la chos sna

111b3(mdo sde): de ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad kyis dus gsum du gtogs pa'i sa'i khams thams cad byin gyis brlabaso chu'i khams thams cad dang / me'i khams thams
111b4(mdo sde): cad dang / rlung gi khams thams cad dang / na mkha'i khams thams cad byin gyis brlab so// de nas sangs rgyas/ bcom ldan 'das de dag thams cad kyis gang dag sangs
111b5(mdo sde): rgyas kyi zhing 'di na gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams dang / brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten skyong ba dang / lha dang / klu dang // 
111b6(mdo sde): gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / na mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po'i dbang po dag dang / gang dag yang gzi brjid che ba'i sems can rnams dang / gang
111b7(mdo sde): ngag yang gling bzhi pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams na gnas pa de dag thams cad la bos te 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// kye grogs po dag sems can thams cad yongasu smin par
111b8(mdo sde): bya ba'i chos kyi tshul 'di byin gyis brlabs te/ khyod kyi la shi tu gtad kyis ci nas 'dir dam pa'i chos 'di myur du mi 'jigs pa dang / nub par mi 'gyur ba de ltar khyod kyis
112a1(mdo sde): dam pa'i chos 'di yid la gyis shig/ 'bar bar gyis shig rigs kyi bu 'am rigs kyi bu mo dad pa gang 'dus pa chen po'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di 'dzin pa nas
112a2(mdo sde): yi ger bris te 'chang ba'i bar du byed pa dang dge slong ngam/ dge slong ma 'am/ dge bsnyen nam/ dge bsnyen ma dang / dam pa'i chos 'dzin pa'i gang zag de dag thams cad yongasu bsrungs/ 
112a3(mdo sde): zhing yongasu bskyabs pa'i phyir rigs par khyod kyi lag tu btad kyis chos smra ba dang / chos la dga' ba dang / bsam gtan la mngon par dga' ba dang / chos mnyan pa dang / dam bI
112a4(mdo sde): chos 'dzin pa'i gang zag rnams khyed kyis bsrung bar bya ba'i phyir yongasu bskyang ba'i bar du gyis shig/ de ci'i phyir zhe na/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang
112a5(mdo sde): dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas gang dag byung bar gyu/ ra pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa de dag thams cad/ kyang nyon mongs pa can snyigs ma lnga dang ldan pa'i sang
112a6(mdo sde): rgyas kyi zhing du 'dus nas/ chos kyi tshul 'ad srung ba dang / mi nub par bya ba dang / dam pa'i chos 'dzin pa'i gang zag kun tu bsrung ba nas/ sems can thams cad yongasu
112a7(mdo sde): smin par bya ba'i bar gyi phyir/ brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten skyong ba thams cad kyi lag tu gtad do// de bzhin du ma 'ongs pa'i dus na/ phyogs bcur sangs rgyas ba
112a8(mdo sde): ldan 'das 'byung ba de dag thams cad kyang nyon mongs pa can snyigs ma lnga dang ldan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing du skad cig gis 'dus te sems can la phan pa'i phyir gzugs
112b1(mdo sde): kyi gsang sngags kyi tshig 'di dag kyang 'chad par 'gyur ro// chos kyi tshul 'di yang byin gyis rlob par 'gyur zhing chos kyi tshul 'di bsrung ba dang / yongasu bskyang ba'i phyir/ brgya
112b2(mdo sde): byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten skyong ba thams cad kyi lag tu gtad par 'gyur ro// de bzhin du nged kyis kyang da ltar kun tu bsrung ba dang / sems can yongasu smin par bya ba'i phyir/ 
112b3(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di na gnas pa rnams dang / gling bzhi pa na gnas pa'i brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten skyong ba dang / lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri zi dang / lha ma
112b4(mdo sde): yin dang / na mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen dpo'i dbang po rnams kyi lag tu 'di shin tu gtad kyi sa ci nas myur du mi 'jig cing nub par mi 'gyur ba de
112b5(mdo sde): ltar khyed kyis dam pa'i chos kyi tshul 'di yid la gyis shi ga/ rab tu 'bar bar gyis shig/ bsrung bar gyis shi/ ga/ rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo dad pa gang dag dang / 
112b6(mdo sde): dam bcas pa'i chos 'dzin pa'i gang zag dge slong dang / dge slong ma dang / dge bsnyen dang / dge bsnyen ma rnams gang 'dus pa chen po'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di 'dzin pa nas tha na
112b7(mdo sde): glegs bam la bris te 'chang bar byed pa'i bar dang / chos smra ba dang / chos nyan pa dang / bsam gtan la mngon par brtson pa dang / dam pa'i chos 'dzin pa de dag la khyed kyis bsrung
112b8(mdo sde): par bya'o// rim gro bya'o// mchod par bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ chos kyi rnam grangs 'di sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs te/ grong ngam/ grong khyer ram/ grong brdal lam/ 
113a1(mdo sde): ljongs sam/ ri brags sam/ pho brang 'khor dang / dgon pa'i gnas nas/ dmangs kyi khyim gyi bar du gang na chos kyi rnam grangs 'di rab tu spyod de/ 'chad dam/ lung 'jog/ 
113a2(mdo sde): gam/ kun chub par bgyid dam/ tha na glegs bam la bris te/ 'chang na/ chos kyi bcud des sa'i bcud dang / sems can gyi mdangs 'phel bar 'gyur te/ khyed des mdangs dang
113a3(mdo sde): ldan zhing / gzi brjid dang stobs brtson 'grus dang / pha rol gnon pa dang ldan par 'gyur/ khyed kyi g.yog 'khor dang / gzhal med khang yang 'phel bar 'gyur/ mi'i rgyal po rnams
113a4(mdo sde): kyang bsrungs par 'gyur te/ de dag gi rgyal srid dang / dbang phyug kyang 'phel bar 'gyur/ de dag gi yul 'khor da thams cad kyang bsrungs par 'gyur// 'dzam bu'i gling gi
113a5(mdo sde): rgyal po rnams kyang chos kyi bcud des tshim nas gcig la gcig phan pa'i sems dang ldan par 'gyur/ rgyal po de dag las kyi rnam par smin pa la yang mngon pa
113a6(mdo sde): yid ches par 'gyur ro// dge ba'i sems su 'gyur/ ser sna med pa'i sems dang / phan pa'i dngos po'i sems dang / sems can thams cad la snying rje ba'i sems nas yang dag
113a7(mdo sde): par lta ba'i bar du 'gyur ro// so so bdag bdag gi yul la mngon par dga' bar 'gyur/ 'dzam bu'i gling 'di yang skye bo rag pas gang bar 'gyur/ shin tu lo legs pa dang / 
113a8(mdo sde): shin tu nyams dga' bar 'gyur/ skye bo mang pos gang zhing sa yang mdangs dang ldan par 'gyur/ 'bras bu shin tu mdog bzang ba dang / shin tu zhom pa dang / lo ma'i sman dang / 
113b1(mdo sde): me tog gi sman dang / nor dang / 'bru rnams shin tu 'byor pa dang / nad med pa dang / bde ba la reg par gnas pa skyed par 'gyuraro// 'thab pa dang / rtsod pa dang / mu ge dang / nad dang / 
113b2(mdo sde): pha rol gyi dmag tshogs dang / dug dang / sha sbrang dang / sbrang bu dang / phye ma leb dang / sbrul gdug pa dang / gnod sbyin dang / srin bu ma rungs pa dang / ri dgas dang / bya dang / spyang ki dang / 
113b3(mdo sde): dus ma yin pa'i rlung dang / char pa rab tu zhi bar 'gyur/ skar ma dang / nyin mo dang / mtshan mo dang / zla ba dang / zla ba phyed dang / lo dang / dus rnams kyang legs par 'byung bar 'gyur/ 
113b4(mdo sde): sems can rnams kyang phal cher dge ba bcu'i las dkyi lam la spyod par 'gyur 'di nas shi 'phos nas kyang / bde 'gro mtho ris kyi 'jig rten du lha rnams kyi
113b5(mdo sde): nang du skye bar 'gyur te/ de dag kyang khyed kyi g.yog tu 'gyuraro// de ltar gzungs kyi phyag rgya'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di'i yon tan mang zhing phan yon che ste/ sems
113b6(mdo sde): can rnams 'khor ba'i pha rol du 'gro bar bya ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyis 'dus pa chen po'i byin gyis brlabs te/ grags pa 'phel zhing yongasu rdzogs par
113b7(mdo sde): 'gyur ro// bud med kyi dngos po skyes nas myong bar 'gyur ba dang / lan grangs gzhan la myong bar 'gyur ba ma lus par yongasu zad par 'gyur ro// mdor na tshe 'di la bud med
113b8(mdo sde): kyi dngos po myong bar 'gyur bar 'phangs pa thams cad byang bar 'gyur te/ mtshams med pa byed pa dang / dam pa'i chos spong ba dang / 'phags pa la bskur pa 'debs
114a1(mdo sde): pa ma gtogs par gzhan lus dang / ngag dang / yid kyi 'bras bu rnam par smin pa'i gnas ngan len de thams cad yongasu byang bar 'gyuraro// gang chos kyi rnam grang/ 
114a2(mdo sde): 'di tha na glegs bam la bris te 'chang na yang 'dus pa chen po sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di'i mthus de'i las dang // 
114a3(mdo sde): nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa ri rab tsam yang byang bar 'gyur/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad la dmigs pa 'phel zhing yongasu rdzogs par 'gyur/ yan lag thams cad yongs su
114a4(mdo sde): rdzogs pa dang / bsam pa thams cad phun sum tshogs pa dang / lus dang / ngag dang / yid kyi legs par spro/ dad pa thams cad 'phel bar 'gyur ba dang / lta ba ngan
114a5(mdo sde): pa thams cad spong ba dang / dag thams cad chos dang 'thun par tshar gcod pa dang / zhi zhing phra ba'i lam thams cad la 'jug par 'gyu ro// yul gang du gzungs
114a6(mdo sde): kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di spyod par 'gyur ba der sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlab pa 'dus pa chen po'i gzungs kyi chos kyi rnam grangs 'di'i mthus sa phyogs
114a7(mdo sde): 'di shin tu snum par 'gyur// 'bras bu mdangs dang ldan pa dang / shin tu zhim pa dang / ro dang ldan par 'gyur/ kha ba dang / tsha ba dang / rtsub pa dang / ro mod pa dor bar 'gyur/ me
114a8(mdo sde): tog dang / 'bras bu shin tu 'byor pa dang / nor dang / 'bru dang / bang ba dang / mdzod dang / rdza phru dang / bya skyogs rnams par 'phel bar 'gyuro// gos dang / zas dang skom dang / sman
114b1(mdo sde): dang / yo byad rnams shin tu 'byor par 'gyur te de na sems can gang dag zas dang / skom gyis 'tsho ba de dag ni shin tu nad med pa dang / nor dang ldan pa dang / kha dog dang ldan pa
114b2(mdo sde): dang / stobs dang ldan pa dang / dran pa dang ldan pa dang / chos 'dod pa dang / dge ba tshol ba la mngon par brtson pa dang / sdig pa'i lta ba yongasu spong bar 'gyur te/ de dag 'di nas
114b3(mdo sde): shi 'phos nas khyed dang skal ba mnyam par skye bar 'gyur te/ de dag gis khyed kyi g.yog 'phel nas stobs dang ldan zhing thogs pa med pa'i tshogs su 'gyur gyis/ chos kyi
114b4(mdo sde): stobs kyis rigs bzhi'i skye bo'i tshogs yongasu bskyed dbar gyis shig/ sems can rnams chos kyi don la chud cig/ de ltar na khyed kyis dus gsum du gshegs

114b6(mdo sde): po'i mdo'i chos kyi tshul 'di bzung ba dang / bshad pa dang bsrung ba'i phyir/ sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi ye shes kyi sgra dbyangs rnam par dag pas don dang / tshig brjod pa'i tshul gyis
114b7(mdo sde): sangs rgyas kyi zhing ma lus pa 'di kun bkang nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams dang / brgya byin gyi dbang po nas/ tshangs pa'i dbang po dang / lto 'phya
114b8(mdo sde): chen po'i dbang po thams cad kyi bar du gang dag sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di na gnas pa phal cher gling bzhi pa 'di na gnas pa rnams la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams
115a1(mdo sde): cad kyi bka' spro ba mdzad do// yang de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po byams pa la sogs pa gang dag bzod pa thob pa bye ba stong phrag dgu
115a2(mdo sde): bcu rtsa bdun sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'di na gnas pa de dag thams cad kyis mgrin gcig tu 'di skad ces gsol to// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das thams cad kyi bkas bdeg
115a3(mdo sde): cag gis kyang dus gsum du gshegs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la mchod pa'i slad du/ chos kyi rnam grangs 'di rigs pas ston par bkur zhing gus pa chen po
115a4(mdo sde): bzung bar bgyi'o// snying rjes sems can yongasu smin par bgyi ba nas/ bla na med pa'i lam gyi bar la dgod pa'i slad du bdag cag gis chos kyi rnam grangs 'di grong
115a5(mdo sde): ngam/ grong khyer dang / grong brdal dang / ljongs dang / yu/ la dang / pho brang 'khor dang / dgon pa'i gnasu rgyas par bstan par bgyi'o// dam pa'i chos yun ring
115a6(mdo sde): du gnas par bgyi ba'i slad du sems can rnams kyang yongasu smin par bgyi'o// yang de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'dir gtogs pa'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das de dag thams
115a7(mdo sde): cad kyis leg so zhes bya ba byin te/ skyes bu dam pa dag legaso leg so// khyod kyis de bzhin gyis shig/ de nas brgya byin dang / tshangs pa nas/ lto 'phye chen po'i dbang po'i bar
115a8(mdo sde): thams cad dang / gang dag gzhan yang sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'dir 'dus pa sems can gzi brjid che ba gzi brjid che ba bye ba khrag khrig phrag drug cu rtsa bzhi de dag thams cad
115b1(mdo sde): kyis mgrin gcig tu 'di skad ces gsol to// bdag cag gis kyang dam pa'i chos yun ring du gnas par bgyi ba'i slad du 'dus pa chen po'i chos kyi rnam grangs 'di
115b2(mdo sde): bzung bar gyi ba nas rgyas par rab tu bshad pa'i bar du bgyi'o// yang dag par bstan par bgyi'o// sems can yong su smin par bgyi'o// chos 'tshal ba dang / chos mnyan

115b8(mdo sde): bzangs dag legaso leg so// khyed kyis de bzhin du gyis shig/ bdag dang gzhan dang / gnyis ka'i phyir nan tan gyis shig/ de ltar na khyed kyis dus gsum du gshegs pa'i

116a2(mdo sde): 'bar bar bya ba dang / dam pa'i chos yun ring du gnas par bya ba'i phyir brtson na/ khyed ring por mi thogs par myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub mngon par
